<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of films considered the best</h1>			<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
				<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>				<div id="contentSub"></div>
				<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>				<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
				<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg/220px-Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg" width="220" height="275" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg/330px-Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg/440px-Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg 2x" data-file-width="984" data-file-height="1230" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Citizen-Kane-Welles-Podium.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Citizen_Kane" title="Citizen Kane">Citizen Kane</a></i> (1941), starring and directed by <a href="/wiki/Orson_Welles" title="Orson Welles">Orson Welles</a>, has topped several international polls, including five <i><a href="/wiki/Sight_%26_Sound" title="Sight &amp; Sound">Sight &amp; Sound</a></i> critics' polls</div></div></div>
<p>This is a list of <b>films considered "the best ever"</b>, so voted in a national or international <a href="/wiki/Opinion_poll" title="Opinion poll">survey</a> of either <a href="/wiki/Film_criticism" title="Film criticism">critics</a> or the public.
</p><p>Some surveys focus on all films, while others focus on a particular genre or country. <a href="/wiki/Electoral_system" title="Electoral system">Voting systems</a> differ from poll to poll: some surveys suffer from biases such as <a href="/wiki/Self-selection_bias" title="Self-selection bias">self-selection</a> or skewed <a href="/wiki/Demography" title="Demography">demographics</a>, while others may be susceptible to forms of interference such as <a href="/wiki/Electoral_fraud#Ballot_stuffing" title="Electoral fraud">vote-stacking</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Critics_and_filmmakers">Critics and filmmakers</span></h2>
<h3><span id="Sight_.26_Sound"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sight_&amp;_Sound"><i>Sight &amp; Sound</i></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg/220px-Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg/330px-Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg/440px-Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1002" data-file-height="566" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vertigo_1958_trailer_Kim_Novak_at_Golden_Gate_Bridge_Fort_Point.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Vertigo_(film)" title="Vertigo (film)"><i>Vertigo</i></a> (1958) was ranked number one in the most recent <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Sight_%26_Sound" title="Sight &amp; Sound">Sight &amp; Sound</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Sight_%26_Sound_Top_50_Greatest_Films_of_All_Time" title="The Sight &amp; Sound Top 50 Greatest Films of All Time">The Sight &amp; Sound Top 50 Greatest Films of All Time</a></div>
<p>Every decade, starting in 1952, the British film magazine <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> asks an international group of film critics to vote for the greatest film of all time. Since 1992, they have invited directors to vote in a separate poll. 63 critics participated in 1952, 70 critics in 1962, 89 critics in 1972, 122 critics in 1982, 132 critics and 101 directors in 1992, 145 critics and 108 directors in 2002, and 846 critics and 358 directors in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This poll is regarded as one of the most important "greatest ever film" lists. American critic <a href="/wiki/Roger_Ebert" title="Roger Ebert">Roger Ebert</a> described it as "by far the most respected of the countless polls of great movies—the only one most serious movie people take seriously."<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Bicycle_Thieves" title="Bicycle Thieves">Bicycle Thieves</a></i> (1948) topped the first poll in 1952 with 25 votes.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Citizen_Kane" title="Citizen Kane">Citizen Kane</a></i> (1941) topped five critics' polls, with 22 votes in 1962, 32 votes in 1972, 45 votes in 1982, 43 votes in 1992, and 46 votes in 2002. It also topped the first two directors' polls, with 30 votes in 1992 and 42 votes in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Vertigo_(film)" title="Vertigo (film)">Vertigo</a></i> (1958) topped the critics' poll in 2012 with 191 votes, dethroning <i>Citizen Kane</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Tokyo_Story" title="Tokyo Story">Tokyo Story</a></i> (1953) topped the directors' poll in 2012 with 48 votes, dethroning <i>Citizen Kane</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_polls">Other polls</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg/220px-Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg" width="220" height="153" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg/330px-Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg/440px-Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="416" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mastroianni_ottomez.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/8%C2%BD" title="8½">8½</a></i> (1963) was the highest-ranked Italian film in many international professional polls</div></div></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Battleship_Potemkin" title="Battleship Potemkin">Battleship Potemkin</a></i> (1925) was ranked number 1 with 32 votes when the Festival Mondial du Film et des Beaux-Arts de Belgique asked 63 film professionals around the world, mostly directors, to vote for the best films of the half-century in 1951.<sup id="cite_ref-Referendum_International_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Referendum_International-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 when the <a href="/wiki/Expo_58" title="Expo 58">Brussels World's Fair</a> polled 117 experts from 26 countries in 1958.<sup id="cite_ref-Expo_58_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Expo_58-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Citizen_Kane" title="Citizen Kane">Citizen Kane</a></i> (1941) was ranked number 1 with 48 votes when French film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Cahiers_du_cin%C3%A9ma" title="Cahiers du cinéma">Cahiers du cinéma</a></i> asked 78 French critics and historians to vote for the best films in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 with 48 votes when Chinese website Cinephilia.net asked 135 Chinese-speaking critics, scholars, curators, and cultural workers to vote for the best films in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> It was ranked number 1 with 49 votes when Spanish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nickel_Odeon_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nickel Odeon (magazine) (page does not exist)">Nickel Odeon</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nickel_Odeon_(revista)" class="extiw" title="es:Nickel Odeon (revista)">es</a>)</span></i> asked 150 Spanish film experts to vote for the best films in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vertigo_(film)" title="Vertigo (film)"><i>Vertigo</i></a> (1958) was ranked number 1 with 39 votes when German film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Steadycam_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Steadycam (magazine) (page does not exist)">Steadycam</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://de.wikipedia.org/wiki/Steadycam_(Filmzeitschrift)" class="extiw" title="de:Steadycam (Filmzeitschrift)">de</a>)</span></i> asked 174 critics and filmmakers to vote for their favorite films in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 with 25 votes when Iranian film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Film_(Iranian_magazine)" title="Film (Iranian magazine)">Film</a></i> asked 92 Iranian critics to vote for the best films in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-Film_(Iran)_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Film_(Iran)-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/8%C2%BD" title="8½">8½</a></i> (1963) was voted the best foreign (i.e. non-Swedish) sound film with 21 votes in a 1964 poll of 50 Swedish film professionals organized by Swedish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Chaplin_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Chaplin (magazine) (page does not exist)">Chaplin</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://sv.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chaplin_(filmtidskrift)" class="extiw" title="sv:Chaplin (filmtidskrift)">sv</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Chaplin_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chaplin-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 when the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Museum_of_Cinematography_in_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Museum of Cinematography in Łódź (page does not exist)">Museum of Cinematography in Łódź</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Kinematografii_w_%C5%81odzi" class="extiw" title="pl:Muzeum Kinematografii w Łodzi">pl</a>)</span> asked 279 Polish film professionals (filmmakers, critics, and professors) to vote for the best films in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-Łódź_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Łódź-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Godfather" title="The Godfather">The Godfather</a></i> (1972) was ranked number 1 when Japanese film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Kinema_Junpo" title="Kinema Junpo">Kinema Junpo</a></i> asked 114 Japanese critics and film professionals to vote for the best foreign (i.e. non-Japanese) films in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-kinejun1_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kinejun1-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the greatest film in a <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hollywood_Reporter" title="The Hollywood Reporter">Hollywood Reporter</a></i> poll of 2120 industry members, including every studio, agency, publicity firm and production house in Hollywood in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-hollywood_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hollywood-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Apocalypse_Now" title="Apocalypse Now">Apocalypse Now</a></i> (1979) was voted number 1 by a group of 3,760 film critics and personalities on the Channel 4 program <i><a href="/wiki/50_Films_to_See_Before_You_Die" title="50 Films to See Before You Die">50 Films to See Before You Die</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Audience_polls">Audience polls</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:211px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Godfather_puppetmaster.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/16/Godfather_puppetmaster.jpg" width="209" height="214" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="209" data-file-height="214" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Godfather_puppetmaster.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/The_Godfather" title="The Godfather">The Godfather</a></i> (1972) tops many audience and professionals polls</div></div></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Gone_with_the_Wind_(film)" title="Gone with the Wind (film)">Gone with the Wind</a></i> (1939) was voted the favorite film of Americans in a poll of 2,279 adults undertaken by <a href="/wiki/Harris_Interactive" class="mw-redirect" title="Harris Interactive">Harris Interactive</a> in 2008,<sup id="cite_ref-Harris_2008_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Harris_2008-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and again in a follow-up poll of 2,276 adults in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-Harris_2014_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Harris_2014-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Roman_Holiday" title="Roman Holiday">Roman Holiday</a></i> (1953) was voted the best foreign (i.e. non-Japanese) film of all time in a 1990 poll of about a million people organized by Japanese public broadcaster <a href="/wiki/NHK" title="NHK">NHK</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-NHK_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NHK-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Godfather" title="The Godfather">The Godfather</a></i> (1972) was voted number 1 by <i><a href="/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly" title="Entertainment Weekly">Entertainment Weekly</a></i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s readers in 1999<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and voted as number 1 in a <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a></i> readers' poll in 1998.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> The film was voted the "Greatest Movie of All Time" in September 2008 by 10,000 readers of <i><a href="/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine)" title="Empire (film magazine)">Empire</a></i> magazine, 150 people from the movie business, and 50 film critics.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> It also topped <i>Empire</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s June 2017 poll of 20,000 readers.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Empire_Strikes_Back" title="The Empire Strikes Back">The Empire Strikes Back</a></i> (1980) was voted the best film of all time by over 250,000 readers of the <i>Empire</i> film magazine in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Shawshank_Redemption" title="The Shawshank Redemption">The Shawshank Redemption</a></i> (1994) was voted the greatest film of all time by Empire magazine readers in "The 201 Greatest Movies of All Time" poll undertaken in March, 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shiri_(film)" title="Shiri (film)"><i>Shiri</i></a> (1999) was voted the favorite film of Koreans with 11,918 votes in a 2002 online poll of 54,013 people conducted by Korean movie channel <a href="/wiki/Orion_Cinema_Network" title="Orion Cinema Network">Orion Cinema Network</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OCN_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OCN-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings_(film_series)" title="The Lord of the Rings (film series)">The <i>Lord of the Rings</i> trilogy</a> (2001–2003) was voted the most popular film of all time by an audience poll for the Australian television special <i><a href="/wiki/My_Favourite_Film" title="My Favourite Film">My Favourite Film</a></i> in 2005<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and by a poll cast by 120,000 German voters for the TV special <i>Die besten Filme aller Zeiten</i> ("The best films of all time") in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Genres_or_media">Genres or media</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Action">Action</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Mad_Max_2" title="Mad Max 2">Mad Max 2</a></i> (1981) was voted the greatest action film of all time in a readers' poll by American magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Die_Hard" title="Die Hard">Die Hard</a></i> (1988) was voted the best action film of all time with 21 votes in a 2014 poll of 50 directors, actors, critics, and experts conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> New York</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span id="Animation_.28shorts_and_features.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Animation_(shorts_and_features)">Animation (shorts and features)</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Pinocchio_(1940_film)" title="Pinocchio (1940 film)">Pinocchio</a></i> (1940) was voted the best animated movie ever made in a 2014 poll of animators, filmmakers, critics, journalists, and experts conducted by <i>Time Out</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/What%27s_Opera,_Doc%3F" title="What&#39;s Opera, Doc?">What's Opera, Doc?</a></i> (1957), a <a href="/wiki/Bugs_Bunny" title="Bugs Bunny">Bugs Bunny</a> cartoon, was selected as the greatest animated short film of all time by 1,000 animation professionals in the book <i><a href="/wiki/The_50_Greatest_Cartoons" title="The 50 Greatest Cartoons">The 50 Greatest Cartoons</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Hedgehog_in_the_Fog" title="Hedgehog in the Fog">Hedgehog in the Fog</a></i> (1975) was ranked number 1 in a poll at the 2003 Laputa Animation Festival where 140 animators from around the world voted for the best animated films of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Tale_of_Tales_(1979_film)" title="Tale of Tales (1979 film)">Tale of Tales</a></i> (1979) was ranked number 1 with 17 votes in a poll at the Olympiad of Animation in 1984 where an international panel of 35 journalists, scholars, festival directors, and animation programmers voted for the best animated films.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Tale_of_Tales_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tale_of_Tales-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 in a poll organized by the <a href="/wiki/Channel_4" title="Channel 4">Channel 4</a> animation magazine <i>Dope Sheet</i> in 1997, as well as a poll organized by the <a href="/wiki/Animafest_Zagreb" title="Animafest Zagreb">Zagreb International Animation Festival</a>, which announced the results in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-Tale_of_Tales_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tale_of_Tales-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Toy_Story" title="Toy Story">Toy Story</a></i> (1995) was voted number 1 on the "Top 100 Animated Features of All Time" list by the <a href="/wiki/Online_Film_Critics_Society" title="Online Film Critics Society">Online Film Critics Society</a> (published March 2003). Voters chose from a reminder list of more than 350 films.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> It also topped a poll of 4000 film fans for "greatest animated film of all time" in 2009, when it was <a href="/wiki/Toy_Story#3-D_re-release" title="Toy Story">re-released in 3D</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Christmas">Christmas</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Die_Hard" title="Die Hard">Die Hard</a></i> (1988) was voted the greatest Christmas movie by British film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine)" title="Empire (film magazine)">Empire</a></i> readers in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Comedy">Comedy</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Some_Like_It_Hot" title="Some Like It Hot">Some Like It Hot</a></i> (1959) was voted the best comedy of all time in a poll of 253 film critics from 52 countries conducted by the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Blazing_Saddles" title="Blazing Saddles">Blazing Saddles</a></i> (1974) was voted the funniest movie of all time in a 2014 readers' poll by <i>Rolling Stone</i> magazine<i>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Monty_Python%27s_Life_of_Brian" title="Monty Python&#39;s Life of Brian">Monty Python's Life of Brian</a></i> (1979) was voted the greatest comedy of all time in a poll of over 22,000 people conducted by the British TV network <a href="/wiki/Channel_4" title="Channel 4">Channel 4</a> in 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the greatest comedy film in polls conducted by British film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Film" title="Total Film">Total Film</a></i> in 2000,<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and British newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/This_Is_Spinal_Tap" title="This Is Spinal Tap">This Is Spinal Tap</a></i> (1984) was voted the best comedy movie of all time in a poll of over 70 stand-up comedians, actors, writers, and directors conducted by <i>Time Out London</i> in 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span id="Comic.2FSuperhero"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Comic/Superhero">Comic/Superhero</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Superman_(1978_film)" title="Superman (1978 film)">Superman</a></i> (1978) was voted the greatest superhero movie in a poll of 1000 British adults conducted by <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Media" title="Virgin Media">Virgin Media</a> in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Dark_Knight_(film)" title="The Dark Knight (film)">The Dark Knight</a></i> (2008) was voted the greatest superhero movie in a reader's poll conducted by American magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a></i> in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Disaster">Disaster</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Poseidon_Adventure_(1972_film)" title="The Poseidon Adventure (1972 film)">The Poseidon Adventure</a></i> (1972) was voted best disaster movie in a poll of 500 members of the <a href="/wiki/UCI_Cinemas" class="mw-redirect" title="UCI Cinemas">UCI Cinemas</a> staff in May 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Documentary">Documentary</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Man_with_a_Movie_Camera" title="Man with a Movie Camera">Man with a Movie Camera</a></i> (1929) was voted the greatest documentary of all time with 125 votes (100 critics and 25 filmmakers) in a <a href="/wiki/Sight_%26_Sound#Greatest_Documentaries_of_All_Time" title="Sight &amp; Sound">2014 Sight &amp; Sound poll</a> of 238 critics, curators, and academics (including many documentary specialists) and 103 filmmakers.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Hoop_Dreams" title="Hoop Dreams">Hoop Dreams</a></i> (1994) was ranked as the greatest documentary of all time by the <a href="/wiki/International_Documentary_Association" title="International Documentary Association">International Documentary Association</a> (IDA) in 2007. Voters selected from a list of over 700 films.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Bowling_for_Columbine" title="Bowling for Columbine">Bowling for Columbine</a></i> (2002) heads the list of 20 all-time favorite non-fiction films selected by members of the IDA in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Horror">Horror</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Exorcist_(film)" title="The Exorcist (film)">The Exorcist</a></i> (1973) was voted the best horror film of all time with 53 votes in a 2012 poll of 150 experts conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> London</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best horror film with 67 votes in a 2015 poll of 104 horror professionals conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/HitFix" title="HitFix">HitFix</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> and topped a readers' poll by <i>Rolling Stone</i> magazine in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Texas_Chain_Saw_Massacre" title="The Texas Chain Saw Massacre">The Texas Chain Saw Massacre</a></i> (1974) was ranked number 1 on British film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Film" title="Total Film">Total Film</a></i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s 2005 list of the greatest horror films.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> In 2010 it was voted into first place in an additional <i>Total Film</i> poll of leading directors and stars of horror films.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Musical">Musical</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/West_Side_Story_(film)" title="West Side Story (film)">West Side Story</a></i> (1961) was chosen as the best screen musical by readers of British newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Observer" title="The Observer">The Observer</a></i> in a 2007 poll.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Rocky_Horror_Picture_Show" title="The Rocky Horror Picture Show">The Rocky Horror Picture Show</a></i> (1975) was voted the best movie musical by readers of <a href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone" title="Rolling Stone">Rolling Stone</a> in a 2017 poll.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romance">Romance</span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Casablanca_(film)" title="Casablanca (film)"><i>Casablanca</i></a> (1942) was voted the best romance film of all time with 56 votes in a 1996 poll of 100 experts organized by Spanish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nickel_Odeon_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nickel Odeon (magazine) (page does not exist)">Nickel Odeon</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nickel_Odeon_(revista)" class="extiw" title="es:Nickel Odeon (revista)">es</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Brief_Encounter" title="Brief Encounter">Brief Encounter</a></i> (1945) was voted the best romance film of all time with 25 votes in a 2013 poll of 101 experts conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> London</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Science_fiction">Science fiction</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_(8999724648).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg/220px-Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg/330px-Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg/440px-Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_%288999724648%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4912" data-file-height="2760" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Stanley_Kubrick_The_Exhibition_-_LACMA_-_2001_A_Space_Odyssey_-_Tycho_moon_crater_model_(8999724648).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/2001:_A_Space_Odyssey_(film)" title="2001: A Space Odyssey (film)">2001: A Space Odyssey</a></i> (1968) was ranked as the best science fiction film in several polls</div></div></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/2001:_A_Space_Odyssey_(film)" title="2001: A Space Odyssey (film)">2001: A Space Odyssey</a></i> (1968) was voted the best <a href="/wiki/Science_fiction_film" title="Science fiction film">science fiction film</a> of all time with 73 votes in a 2014 poll of 136 science fiction  experts, filmmakers, science fiction writers, film critics, and scientists conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> London</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> It was voted the best science fiction film of all time by 115 members of the <a href="/wiki/Online_Film_Critics_Society" title="Online Film Critics Society">Online Film Critics Society</a> in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> It topped a readers' poll conducted by <i>Rolling Stone</i> magazine in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> It is also the only science fiction film to make the <i><a href="/wiki/Sight_%26_Sound" title="Sight &amp; Sound">Sight &amp; Sound</a></i> critics' poll for the ten best movies (number 10 in 1992, number 6 in 2002 and 2012).<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Blade_Runner" title="Blade Runner">Blade Runner</a></i> (1982) was voted the best science fiction film by a panel of 56 scientists assembled by the British newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> In British magazine <i><a href="/wiki/New_Scientist" title="New Scientist">New Scientist</a></i>, <i>Blade Runner</i> was voted "all-time favourite science fiction film" in the readers' poll in 2008, with 12 percent of thousands of votes.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> It topped a 2011 poll by <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Film" title="Total Film">Total Film</a></i> magazine.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Serenity_(2005_film)" title="Serenity (2005 film)">Serenity</a></i> (2005) was voted the best science fiction movie in a poll of 3,000 people conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/SFX_(magazine)" title="SFX (magazine)">SFX</a></i> magazine.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Silent">Silent</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Battleship_Potemkin" title="Battleship Potemkin">Battleship Potemkin</a></i> (1925) was voted the best silent film with 32 votes in a 1964 poll of 50 Swedish film professionals organized by Swedish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Chaplin_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Chaplin (magazine) (page does not exist)">Chaplin</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://sv.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chaplin_(filmtidskrift)" class="extiw" title="sv:Chaplin (filmtidskrift)">sv</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Chaplin_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chaplin-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Rocky" title="Rocky">Rocky</a></i> (1976) topped British website <a href="/wiki/Digital_Spy" title="Digital Spy">Digital Spy</a>'s "greatest ever sports movie" online poll in 2012, with 18.7% of the votes. Voters chose from a list of 25 films.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="War">War</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Saving_Private_Ryan" title="Saving Private Ryan">Saving Private Ryan</a></i> (1998) was voted as the greatest war film in a 2008 <a href="/wiki/Channel_4" title="Channel 4">Channel 4</a> poll of the 100 greatest war films.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Western">Western</span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Stagecoach_(1939_film)" title="Stagecoach (1939 film)"><i>Stagecoach</i></a> (1939) was voted the best western film of all time with 54 votes in a 1996 poll of 100 experts organized by Spanish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nickel_Odeon_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nickel Odeon (magazine) (page does not exist)">Nickel Odeon</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nickel_Odeon_(revista)" class="extiw" title="es:Nickel Odeon (revista)">es</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Johnny_Guitar" title="Johnny Guitar">Johnny Guitar</a></i> (1954) was the most cited film in the "Ten Best Westerns" lists of 27 French critics in <i>Le Western</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="National_polls">National polls</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Argentina">Argentina</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Argentina" title="Cinema of Argentina">Cinema of Argentina</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Chronicle_of_a_Boy_Alone" title="Chronicle of a Boy Alone">Crónica de un niño solo</a></i> (1965) was voted the best Argentine film of all time in a 2000 poll of critics and film historians organized by the <a href="/wiki/Museo_del_Cine_Pablo_Ducros_Hicken" title="Museo del Cine Pablo Ducros Hicken">Museo del Cine Pablo Ducros Hicken</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Australia" title="Cinema of Australia">Cinema of Australia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Picnic_at_Hanging_Rock_(film)" title="Picnic at Hanging Rock (film)">Picnic at Hanging Rock</a></i> (1975) was voted the best Australian film of all time by members of the Australian Film Institute, industry guilds and unions, film critics and reviewers, academics and media teachers, and Kookaburra Card members of the <a href="/wiki/National_Film_and_Sound_Archive" title="National Film and Sound Archive">National Film and Sound Archive</a> (NFSA), in a 1996 poll organized by the Victorian Centenary of Cinema Committee and the NFSA.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Castle_(1997_Australian_film)" title="The Castle (1997 Australian film)">The Castle</a></i> (1997) was selected by the public as Australia's favourite film in a 2008 online poll conducted by the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Film_Institute" title="Australian Film Institute">Australian Film Institute</a>, in collaboration with <a href="/wiki/Australia_Post" title="Australia Post">Australia Post</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Bangladesh" title="Cinema of Bangladesh">Cinema of Bangladesh</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Titash_Ekti_Nadir_Naam" title="Titash Ekti Nadir Naam">Titash Ekti Nadir Naam</a></i> (1973) topped the list of 10 best Bangladeshi films in the audience and critics' polls conducted by the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a> in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bosnia_and_Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_Bosnia_and_Herzegovina_films" title="List of Bosnia and Herzegovina films">List of Bosnia and Herzegovina films</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Do_You_Remember_Dolly_Bell%3F" title="Do You Remember Dolly Bell?">Do You Remember Dolly Bell?</a></i> (1981) was voted the best Bosnian film of all time in a 2003 poll of 13 film professionals organized by The National Film Archive of Bosnia and Herzegovina.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil">Brazil</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Brazil" title="Cinema of Brazil">Cinema of Brazil</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Limite" class="mw-redirect" title="Limite">Limite</a></i> (1931) is ranked number 1 on the <a href="/wiki/Abraccine_Top_100_Brazilian_films" title="Abraccine Top 100 Brazilian films">Brazilian Film Critics Association's list of the top 100 Brazilian films</a>, voted by its 100 members in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Black_God,_White_Devil" title="Black God, White Devil">Black God, White Devil</a></i> (1964) was voted the best Brazilian film of all time in a 2001 poll of 108 critics and film professionals organized by Brazilian film magazine <i>Contracampo</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Red_Light_Bandit" title="The Red Light Bandit">The Red Light Bandit</a></i> (1968) was voted the best Brazilian film of all time in a 2011 poll of 102 critics, researchers, and professionals organized by Brazilian film magazine <i>Filme Cultura</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Canada" title="Cinema of Canada">Cinema of Canada</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Mon_oncle_Antoine" title="Mon oncle Antoine">Mon oncle Antoine</a></i> (1971) was named first in the <a href="/wiki/Toronto_International_Film_Festival" title="Toronto International Film Festival">Toronto International Film Festival</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Top_10_Canadian_Films_of_All_Time" title="Top 10 Canadian Films of All Time">Top 10 Canadian Films of All Time</a> in 1984, 1993 and 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Sweet_Hereafter_(film)" title="The Sweet Hereafter (film)">The Sweet Hereafter</a></i> (1997) was voted the best Canadian film by readers of <i><a href="/wiki/Playback_(magazine)" title="Playback (magazine)">Playback</a></i> in 2002 in an online poll. More than 500 industry respondents participated in the poll.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Atanarjuat:_The_Fast_Runner" title="Atanarjuat: The Fast Runner">Atanarjuat: The Fast Runner</a></i> (2001) was voted the best Canadian film of all time with 94 votes in a 2015 poll of 220 filmmakers, critics, programmers, and academics organized by the <a href="/wiki/Toronto_International_Film_Festival" title="Toronto International Film Festival">Toronto International Film Festival</a>, dethroning <i>Mon oncle Antoine</i> which won the previous three polls.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chile">Chile</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Chile" title="Cinema of Chile">Cinema of Chile</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Jackal_of_Nahueltoro" title="Jackal of Nahueltoro">Jackal of Nahueltoro</a></i> (1975) was voted the best Chilean film of all time with 57 votes in a 2016 poll of 77 directors, actors, programmers, scholars, journalists, and critics organized by CineChile.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Julio_comienza_en_julio" title="Julio comienza en julio">Julio comienza en julio</a></i> (1979) was chosen in 1999 as the "Best Chilean Film of the Century" in a vote organized by the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_(commune)" title="Santiago (commune)">Municipality of Santiago</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_China" title="Cinema of China">Cinema of China</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Spring_in_a_Small_Town" title="Spring in a Small Town">Spring in a Small Town</a></i> (小城之春; 1948) was ranked number 1 on the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Award" title="Hong Kong Film Award">Hong Kong Film Awards</a> Association's <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Award#Best_100_Chinese_Motion_Pictures" title="Hong Kong Film Award">Best 100 Chinese Motion Pictures</a> list in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-HKFA_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HKFA-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best Chinese film of all time with 25 votes in a 2010 poll of 37 critics organized by the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Critics_Society" title="Hong Kong Film Critics Society">Hong Kong Film Critics Society</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HKFCS_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HKFCS-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Farewell_My_Concubine_(film)" title="Farewell My Concubine (film)">Farewell My Concubine</a></i> (霸王别姬; 1993) was voted the best Mainland Chinese film of all time by 88 international film experts in a poll conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> Shanghai</i> and <i>Time Out Beijing</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Colombia">Colombia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Colombia" title="Cinema of Colombia">Cinema of Colombia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Strategy_of_the_Snail" title="The Strategy of the Snail">The Strategy of the Snail</a></i> (1993) was voted the best Colombian film of all time with 38 votes in a 2015 poll of 65 critics and journalists organized by Colombian magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Semana" title="Semana">Semana</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Croatia">Croatia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Croatia" title="Cinema of Croatia">Cinema of Croatia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Tko_pjeva_zlo_ne_misli" class="mw-redirect" title="Tko pjeva zlo ne misli">Tko pjeva zlo ne misli</a></i> (<i>One Who Sings Means No Harm</i>, 1970) was voted the best Croatian film of all time by 44 Croatian film critics in 1999, in a poll organized by the Croatian magazine <i>Hollywood</i>. It was also voted the best Croatian film by <i>Hollywood</i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s readers.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">Cuba</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Cuba" title="Cinema of Cuba">Cinema of Cuba</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Memories_of_Underdevelopment" title="Memories of Underdevelopment">Memories of Underdevelopment</a></i> (1968) was voted the best Latin American film of all time with 30 votes in a 1999 poll of 36 critics and film specialists from 11 countries organized by critics Carlos Galiano and Rufo Caballero.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best <a href="/wiki/Ibero-America" title="Ibero-America">Ibero-American</a> film of all time in a 2009 poll of more than 500 film professionals, critics, journalists, festival organizers, and fans around the world organized by Spanish magazine <i>Noticine</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</span></h3>
<p><i>See also <a href="#Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</a> and <a href="#Slovakia">Slovakia</a>, below</i>.
</p>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Marketa_Lazarova" class="mw-redirect" title="Marketa Lazarova">Marketa Lazarova</a></i> (1967) was voted the best Czech-Slovak film of all-time in a 1998 poll of 55 Czech and Slovak film critics and publicists, receiving 41 votes.<sup id="cite_ref-CZSK_95-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CZSK-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Firemen%27s_Ball" title="The Firemen&#39;s Ball">The Firemen's Ball</a></i> (1967) was voted the best Czech-Slovak film of all time with 33 votes in a 2007 poll of 53 experts (mostly from the Czech Republic, but also from Slovakia and Poland) titled "Filmové dědictví česko-slovenské kinematografie".<sup id="cite_ref-nostalghia2007_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nostalghia2007-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Elementary_School" title="The Elementary School">The Elementary School</a></i> (1991) was voted the best Czech-Slovak film with 192 votes in a 2007 public poll of "Filmové dědictví česko-slovenské kinematografie".<sup id="cite_ref-nostalghia2007_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nostalghia2007-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="Cinema of the Czech Republic">Cinema of the Czech Republic</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Czech_films_considered_the_best" title="List of Czech films considered the best">List of Czech films considered the best</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Kristi%C3%A1n_(film)" class="mw-redirect" title="Kristián (film)">Christian</a></i> (1939) was voted best Czech film of all time in a poll held by Media Desk and <i>Týden</i> magazine in 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-Poll:_best_Czech_film_of_all_time_is_1939_Kristián_Radio_Prague_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Poll:_best_Czech_film_of_all_time_is_1939_Kristián_Radio_Prague-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Marketa_Lazarova" class="mw-redirect" title="Marketa Lazarova">Marketa Lazarova</a></i> (1967) was voted the best Czech film of all time by Czech journalists during the <a href="/wiki/Karlovy_Vary_International_Film_Festival" title="Karlovy Vary International Film Festival">Karlovy Vary International Film Festival</a> in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> It also topped 1998 poll of Czech and Slovak film critics and publicists during the 1998 Karlovy Vary International Film Festival.<sup id="cite_ref-Markéta_Lazarová_vyhrála_anketu_kritiků_102-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Markéta_Lazarová_vyhrála_anketu_kritiků-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Firemen%27s_Ball" title="The Firemen&#39;s Ball">The Firemen's Ball</a></i> (1967) was voted the best Czech film in a 2018 poll of 20 Czech historians, theorists and critics.<sup id="cite_ref-Století_českého_filmu._Vybíráme_kanonická_díla_moderní_české_státnosti_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Století_českého_filmu._Vybíráme_kanonická_díla_moderní_české_státnosti-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Cosy_Dens" title="Cosy Dens">Cosy Dens</a></i> (1999) was voted the best Czech film with 622 votes in a readers' poll by <i>Reflex</i> magazine in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><i>See also <a href="#Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a>, above.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Egypt">Egypt</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Egypt" title="Cinema of Egypt">Cinema of Egypt</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Night_of_Counting_the_Years" title="The Night of Counting the Years">The Night of Counting the Years</a></i> (1969) was voted the best Arab film of all time (i.e. the best film made in an <a href="/wiki/List_of_Arab_countries_by_population" title="List of Arab countries by population">Arab country</a>) in a 2013 poll of 475 film critics, writers, novelists, academics, and other arts professionals organized by the <a href="/wiki/Dubai_International_Film_Festival" title="Dubai International Film Festival">Dubai International Film Festival</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Estonia">Estonia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Estonia" title="Cinema of Estonia">Cinema of Estonia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Spring_(1969_film)" title="Spring (1969 film)">Kevade</a></i> (<i>Spring</i>, 1969) received first place in the Estonian feature films Top Ten Poll in 2002 held by Estonian film critics and journalists.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Autumn_Ball" title="Autumn Ball">Autumn Ball</a></i> (2007) was voted the best Estonian film of all time with 29 votes in a 2011 poll of 33 film writers and film scholars organized by the Estonian Association of Film Journalists.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Finland">Finland</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Finland" title="Cinema of Finland">Cinema of Finland</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Unknown_Soldier_(1955_film)" title="The Unknown Soldier (1955 film)">The Unknown Soldier</a></i> (1955) was voted the best Finnish movie by 1213 respondents in an Internet poll by <i><a href="/wiki/Helsingin_Sanomat" title="Helsingin Sanomat">Helsingin Sanomat</a></i> in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Komisario_Palmun_erehdys" title="Komisario Palmun erehdys">Komisario Palmun erehdys</a></i> (1960) was chosen as the best Finnish fictional movie of all time in a poll of 48 critics by <a href="/wiki/Yle" title="Yle">Yle</a> in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="France">France</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_France" title="Cinema of France">Cinema of France</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Rules_of_the_Game" title="The Rules of the Game">The Rules of the Game</a></i> (1939) was voted the best French film of all time with 15 votes in a 2012 poll of 85 film professionals conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_(magazine)" title="Time Out (magazine)">Time Out</a> Paris</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> It was voted the best European film of all time with 56 votes (tied with the German film <i><a href="/wiki/Nosferatu" title="Nosferatu">Nosferatu</a></i>) in a 1994 poll of 70 critics and film historians organized by <a href="/wiki/Cinemateca_Portuguesa" title="Cinemateca Portuguesa">Cinemateca Portuguesa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cinemateca_Portuguesa_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cinemateca_Portuguesa-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> It is also the only film that ranked in the top 10 of every <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Georgia">Georgia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Georgia" title="Cinema of Georgia">Cinema of Georgia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Eliso" title="Eliso">Eliso</a></i> (1928) was voted the best Georgian film of all time in a critic poll organized by Tbilisi Intermedia.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Germany">Germany</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Germany" title="Cinema of Germany">Cinema of Germany</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Nosferatu" title="Nosferatu">Nosferatu</a></i> (1922) was voted the best European film of all time with 56 votes (tied with the French film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Rules_of_the_Game" title="The Rules of the Game">The Rules of the Game</a></i>) in a 1994 poll of 70 critics and film historians organized by <a href="/wiki/Cinemateca_Portuguesa" title="Cinemateca Portuguesa">Cinemateca Portuguesa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cinemateca_Portuguesa_112-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cinemateca_Portuguesa-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/M_(1931_film)" title="M (1931 film)">M</a></i> (1931) was voted the best German film of all time with 306 votes in a 1994 poll of 324 film journalists, film critics, filmmakers, and cineastes organized by the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Association_of_German_Cin%C3%A9math%C3%A8ques&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Association of German Cinémathèques (page does not exist)">Association of German Cinémathèques</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://de.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deutscher_Kinematheksverbund" class="extiw" title="de:Deutscher Kinematheksverbund">de</a>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Greece">Greece</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Greece" title="Cinema of Greece">Cinema of Greece</a></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Ogre_of_Athens" title="The Ogre of Athens"><i>O Drakos</i></a> (1956) was voted the best Greek film of all time by members of the <a href="/wiki/Greek_Film_Critics_Association" title="Greek Film Critics Association">Greek Film Critics Association</a> in 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-PEKK_115-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PEKK-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Evdokia_(film)" title="Evdokia (film)"><i>Evdokia</i></a> (1971) was voted the best Greek film of all time by members of the <a href="/wiki/Greek_Film_Critics_Association" title="Greek Film Critics Association">Greek Film Critics Association</a> in 1986.<sup id="cite_ref-PEKK_115-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PEKK-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Hong_Kong" title="Cinema of Hong Kong">Cinema of Hong Kong</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/A_Better_Tomorrow" title="A Better Tomorrow">A Better Tomorrow</a></i> (英雄本色; 1986), filmed and produced in Hong Kong, was voted <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Awards#Best_100_Chinese_Motion_Pictures" class="mw-redirect" title="Hong Kong Film Awards">the second best Chinese film ever made</a> by the Hong Kong Film Awards Association in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-HKFA_88-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HKFA-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Days_of_Being_Wild" title="Days of Being Wild">Days of Being Wild</a></i> (阿飛正傳; 1990) was voted the best Hong Kong film of all time with 16 votes in a 2010 poll of 37 critics organized by the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Critics_Society" title="Hong Kong Film Critics Society">Hong Kong Film Critics Society</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HKFCS_89-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HKFCS-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungary">Hungary</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Hungary" title="Cinema of Hungary">Cinema of Hungary</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Round-Up_(1965_film)" class="mw-redirect" title="The Round-Up (1965 film)">The Round-Up</a></i> (1965) was chosen as the best Hungarian film in a 2000 Hungarian film critics' poll.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/S%C3%A1t%C3%A1ntang%C3%B3" title="Sátántangó">Satan's Tango</a></i> (1994) is 36th, the highest rank for a Hungarian film, in the 2012 <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_India" title="Cinema of India">Cinema of India</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Pather_Panchali" title="Pather Panchali">Pather Panchali</a></i> (1955) is the highest-ranking Indian film on any <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> poll at number 6 in the 1992 Critics' Poll.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It also topped the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a>'s user poll of "Top 10 Indian Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Mayabazar" title="Mayabazar">Mayabazar</a></i> (1957) was chosen as the greatest Indian film of all time with 16,960 votes in an online poll conducted by <a href="/wiki/IBN_Live" class="mw-redirect" title="IBN Live">IBN Live</a> in 2013. Voters select from a list of 100 films from different Indian languages, and 70,926 votes were cast.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Sholay" title="Sholay">Sholay</a></i> (1975) topped the British Film Institute's critics' poll of "Top 10 Indian Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Iran">Iran</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Iran" title="Cinema of Iran">Cinema of Iran</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Deers_(1974_film)" class="mw-redirect" title="The Deers (1974 film)">The Deers</a></i> (1974) was voted the best Iranian film of all time with 33 votes in a 2009 poll of 92 critics organized by Iranian film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Film_(Iranian_magazine)" title="Film (Iranian magazine)">Film</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Film_(Iran)_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Film_(Iran)-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Bashu,_the_Little_Stranger" title="Bashu, the Little Stranger">Bashu, the Little Stranger</a></i> (1986) was voted "Best Iranian Film of all time" in November 1999 by a Persian movie magazine <i>Picture World</i> poll of 150 Iranian critics and professionals.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ireland">Ireland</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Ireland" title="Cinema of Ireland">Cinema of Ireland</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Commitments_(film)" title="The Commitments (film)">The Commitments</a></i> (1991) was voted the best Irish film of all time in a 2005 <a href="/wiki/Jameson_Whiskey" class="mw-redirect" title="Jameson Whiskey">Jameson Whiskey</a> online poll of over 10,000 Irish people.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Israel">Israel</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Israel" title="Cinema of Israel">Cinema of Israel</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Giv%27at_Halfon_Eina_Ona" title="Giv&#39;at Halfon Eina Ona">Giv'at Halfon Eina Ona</a></i> (1976) was voted "Favorite Israeli Film of All Time" in a 2004 poll by Ynet, the platform of the Israeli newspaper <a href="/wiki/Yediot_Ahronot" class="mw-redirect" title="Yediot Ahronot">Yediot Ahronot</a>. The film received votes from 25,000 web users.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Avanti_Popolo_(1986_film)" title="Avanti Popolo (1986 film)">Avanti Popolo</a></i> (1986) was voted "Greatest Israeli Film of All Time" in a 2013 poll of 20 Israeli film experts by <a href="/wiki/Maariv_(newspaper)" title="Maariv (newspaper)">NRG Ma'ariv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Italy">Italy</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Italy" title="Cinema of Italy">Cinema of Italy</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Bicycle_Thieves" title="Bicycle Thieves">Bicycle Thieves</a></i> (1948) topped the first <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll in 1952.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/8%C2%BD" title="8½">8½</a></i> (1963) was voted the best foreign (i.e. non-Swedish) sound film with 21 votes in a 1964 poll of 50 Swedish film professionals organized by Swedish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Chaplin_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Chaplin (magazine) (page does not exist)">Chaplin</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://sv.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chaplin_(filmtidskrift)" class="extiw" title="sv:Chaplin (filmtidskrift)">sv</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Chaplin_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chaplin-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked number 1 when the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Museum_of_Cinematography_in_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Museum of Cinematography in Łódź (page does not exist)">Museum of Cinematography in Łódź</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Kinematografii_w_%C5%81odzi" class="extiw" title="pl:Muzeum Kinematografii w Łodzi">pl</a>)</span> asked 279 Polish film professionals (filmmakers, critics, and professors) to vote for the best films in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-Łódź_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Łódź-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> It also ranked in the top 10, and was the highest ranked Italian film, in the <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll in 1972, 1982, 2002, and 2012, and the directors' poll in 1992, 2002, and 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Japan">Japan</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:So_Yamamura_3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/So_Yamamura_3.jpg/220px-So_Yamamura_3.jpg" width="220" height="164" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/So_Yamamura_3.jpg/330px-So_Yamamura_3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/74/So_Yamamura_3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="411" data-file-height="306" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:So_Yamamura_3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Tokyo_Story" title="Tokyo Story">Tokyo Story</a></i> (1953) topped several international polls</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Japan" title="Cinema of Japan">Cinema of Japan</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Tokyo_Story" title="Tokyo Story">Tokyo Story</a></i> (東京物語; 1953) topped the <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> directors' poll with 48 votes and was number 3 in the critics' poll with 107 votes in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best Japanese film of all time in a 2009 poll of 114 critics and film professionals organized by Japanese film magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Kinema_Junpo" title="Kinema Junpo">Kinema Junpo</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-kinejun1_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kinejun1-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> It was voted the best Asian film of all time in a 2015 poll of 73 film critics, festival executives, programmers, and directors from around the world, organized by the <a href="/wiki/Busan_International_Film_Festival" title="Busan International Film Festival">Busan International Film Festival</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Seven_Samurai" title="Seven Samurai">Seven Samurai</a></i> (1954) was voted the best Japanese film of all time in a 1989 poll of 372 celebrities for a book published by <a href="/wiki/Bungeishunj%C5%AB" title="Bungeishunjū">Bungeishunjū</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> It was voted the best Japanese film of all time in a 1990 poll of about a million people organized by <a href="/wiki/NHK" title="NHK">NHK</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-NHK_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NHK-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> It was also number 3 with 15 votes, the highest ranked Japanese film, in the 1982 <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll. It was also ranked joint tenth on the <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> directors' poll in 1992, and joint ninth in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Rashomon" title="Rashomon">Rashomon</a></i> (1950) was ranked joint tenth in the 1992 <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> directors' poll, and joint ninth in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">Mexico</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Mexico" title="Cinema of Mexico">Cinema of Mexico</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Let%27s_Go_with_Pancho_Villa" title="Let&#39;s Go with Pancho Villa">Vámonos con Pancho Villa</a></i> (1935) was ranked number 1 Mexican film of all time in a 1994 poll of 25 critics and journalists organized by Mexican magazine <i>Somos</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-MEX_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MEX-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands">Netherlands</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_Netherlands" title="Cinema of the Netherlands">Cinema of the Netherlands</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Turkish_Delight_(1973_film)" title="Turkish Delight (1973 film)">Turkish Delight</a></i> (1973) was voted the best Dutch film of all time in a 1999 poll.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Zwartboek" class="mw-redirect" title="Zwartboek">Zwartboek</a></i> (<i>Black Book</i>, 2006) was voted the best Dutch film of all time at the 2008 <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_Film_Festival" title="Netherlands Film Festival">Netherlands Film Festival</a> by nearly 15,000 members of the public.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_New_Zealand" title="Cinema of New Zealand">Cinema of New Zealand</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Once_Were_Warriors_(film)" title="Once Were Warriors (film)">Once Were Warriors</a></i> (1994) was voted the best New Zealand film of all time in a 2014 online poll organized by <a href="/wiki/Fairfax_Media" title="Fairfax Media">Fairfax Media</a>. More than 500 people voted, including about 100 film professionals and 15 critics.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Norway">Norway</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Norway" title="Cinema of Norway">Cinema of Norway</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Nine_Lives_(1957_film)" title="Nine Lives (1957 film)">Ni Liv</a></i> (<i>Nine Lives</i>, 1957) was the critics' choice for "Best Norwegian Film of All Time" during the 2005 Bergen International Film Festival.<sup id="cite_ref-Norway_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Norway-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Chasers_(1959_film)" title="The Chasers (1959 film)">The Chasers</a></i> (1959) was voted the best Norwegian film of all time with 23 votes in a 2011 poll of 32 critics and experts organized by Norwegian film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Rushprint&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Rushprint (page does not exist)">Rushprint</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rushprint" class="extiw" title="no:Rushprint">no</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Fl%C3%A5klypa_Grand_Prix" class="mw-redirect" title="Flåklypa Grand Prix">Flåklypa Grand Prix</a></i> (<i>Pinchcliffe Grand Prix</i>, 1975) was the people's choice for "Best Norwegian Film of All Time" during the 2005 Bergen International Film Festival.<sup id="cite_ref-Norway_132-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Norway-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan">Pakistan</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Pakistan" title="Cinema of Pakistan">Cinema of Pakistan</a></div>
<ul><li><i>Baji</i> (1963) topped the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a>'s critics' poll of "Top 10 Pakistani Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Aina_(1977_film)" title="Aina (1977 film)">Aina</a></i> (1977) topped the British Film Institute's user poll of "Top 10 Pakistani Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">Philippines</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_Philippines" title="Cinema of the Philippines">Cinema of the Philippines</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Manila_in_the_Claws_of_Light" title="Manila in the Claws of Light">Manila in the Claws of Light</a></i> (1975) was voted the best Filipino film of all time with 16 votes (tied with <i><a href="/wiki/Ganito_Kami_Noon,_Paano_Kayo_Ngayon" title="Ganito Kami Noon, Paano Kayo Ngayon">Ganito Kami Noon, Paano Kayo Ngayon</a></i>) in a 1989 poll of 28 filmmakers and critics, organized by Joel David and his UP film criticism class, and published in Philippine magazine <i>National Midweek</i>. The article also included a list of the most common number-one choices (topped by <i><a href="/wiki/Manila_in_the_Claws_of_Light" title="Manila in the Claws of Light">Manila in the Claws of Light</a></i>), as well as an alternate version of the top 10 (topped by <i><a href="/wiki/Manila_by_Night" title="Manila by Night">Manila by Night</a></i>) which was ordered by average rank.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Himala" title="Himala">Himala</a></i> (<i>Miracle</i>, 1982) won the 2008 CNN Asia Pacific Screen Awards Viewers Choice as "Best Asia-Pacific Film of All Time" (voted for by thousands of film fans around the world).<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Poland">Poland</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Poland" title="Cinema of Poland">Cinema of Poland</a></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Promised_Land_(1975_film)" title="The Promised Land (1975 film)"><i>The Promised Land</i></a> (1975) was voted the best Polish film of all time in a 2015 poll of 279 Polish film professionals organized by the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Museum_of_Cinematography_in_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Museum of Cinematography in Łódź (page does not exist)">Museum of Cinematography in Łódź</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muzeum_Kinematografii_w_%C5%81odzi" class="extiw" title="pl:Muzeum Kinematografii w Łodzi">pl</a>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Łódź_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Łódź-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Teddy_Bear_(1980_film)" title="Teddy Bear (1980 film)">Teddy Bear</a></i> (1980) was voted by the public of 2013 Filmfest PL as the best movie of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romania">Romania</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Romania" title="Cinema of Romania">Cinema of Romania</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Reenactment" title="The Reenactment">Reconstituirea</a></i> (<i>The Reenactment</i>, 1968) was selected as the best Romanian film by 40 film critics in 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">Russia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Russia" title="Cinema of Russia">Cinema of Russia</a></div>
