<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/My_Friend_Ivan_Lapshin" title="My Friend Ivan Lapshin">My Friend Ivan Lapshin</a></i> (1985) was voted the best Russian film of all time with 47 votes in a 2008 poll of 100 filmmakers and critics, organized by Russian film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Seance_(Magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Seance (Magazine) (page does not exist)">Seance</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%B0%D0%BD%D1%81_(%D0%B6%D1%83%D1%80%D0%BD%D0%B0%D0%BB)" class="extiw" title="ru:Сеанс (журнал)">ru</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><i>See also <a href="#Soviet_Union">Soviet Union</a>, below</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbia">Serbia</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Who_Sings_Over_There" class="mw-redirect" title="Who Sings Over There">Who Sings Over There</a></i> (1980) was voted by Serbian critics the best Serbian film of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovakia">Slovakia</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Slovakia" title="Cinema of Slovakia">Cinema of Slovakia</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Pictures_of_the_Old_World" title="Pictures of the Old World">Pictures of the Old World</a></i> (1972) was voted the best Slovak film of all time by Slovak critics in 2000.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><i>See also <a href="#Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a>, above.</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovenia">Slovenia</span></h3>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Dancing_in_the_Rain_(film)" title="Dancing in the Rain (film)">Dancing in the Rain</a></i> (1961) was voted the best Slovenian film of all time in a poll by Slovenian critics.<sup id="cite_ref-Slovenian_New_Wave_-_Canadian_Film_Institute_-_Institut_canadien_du_film_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Slovenian_New_Wave_-_Canadian_Film_Institute_-_Institut_canadien_du_film-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Korea">South Korea</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_South_Korea" title="Cinema of South Korea">Cinema of South Korea</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Obaltan" title="Obaltan">Obaltan</a></i> (1961) was voted the best Korean film of all time with 48 votes in a 1999 poll of 140 filmmakers organized by Korean newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Chosun_Ilbo" title="The Chosun Ilbo">The Chosun Ilbo</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best Korean film of all time (tied with <a href="/wiki/The_Housemaid_(1960_film)" title="The Housemaid (1960 film)"><i>The Housemaid</i></a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=The_March_of_Fools_(film)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="The March of Fools (film) (page does not exist)"><i>The March of Fools</i></a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/%EB%B0%94%EB%B3%B4%EB%93%A4%EC%9D%98_%ED%96%89%EC%A7%84_(%EC%98%81%ED%99%94)" class="extiw" title="ko:바보들의 행진 (영화)">ko</a>)</span>) in a 2014 poll of 62 film scholars, critics, film professionals, researchers, and programmers organized by the <a href="/wiki/Korean_Film_Archive" title="Korean Film Archive">Korean Film Archive</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shiri_(film)" title="Shiri (film)"><i>Shiri</i></a> (1999) was voted the favorite film of Koreans with 11,918 votes in a 2002 online poll of 54,013 people conducted by Korean movie channel <a href="/wiki/Orion_Cinema_Network" title="Orion Cinema Network">Orion Cinema Network</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OCN_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OCN-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Memories_of_Murder" title="Memories of Murder">Memories of Murder</a></i> (2003) was voted the best Korean film of all time with 806 votes in a 2014 audience poll of 1462 people organized by the <a href="/wiki/Korean_Film_Archive" title="Korean Film Archive">Korean Film Archive</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Soviet_Union">Soviet Union</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Odessastepsbaby.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Odessastepsbaby.jpg/220px-Odessastepsbaby.jpg" width="220" height="174" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Odessastepsbaby.jpg/330px-Odessastepsbaby.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Odessastepsbaby.jpg/440px-Odessastepsbaby.jpg 2x" data-file-width="912" data-file-height="720" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Odessastepsbaby.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Battleship_Potemkin" title="Battleship Potemkin">Battleship Potemkin</a></i> (1925) was an early favorite and the top <a href="/wiki/Silent_film" title="Silent film">silent film</a></div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Cinema of the Soviet Union">Cinema of the Soviet Union</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Battleship_Potemkin" title="Battleship Potemkin">Battleship Potemkin</a></i> (1925) was ranked number 1 with 32 votes when the Festival Mondial du Film et des Beaux-Arts de Belgique asked 63 film professionals around the world, mostly directors, to vote for the best films of the half-century in 1951.<sup id="cite_ref-Referendum_International_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Referendum_International-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> It was ranked number 1 when the <a href="/wiki/Expo_58" title="Expo 58">Brussels World's Fair</a> polled 117 experts from 26 countries in 1958.<sup id="cite_ref-Expo_58_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Expo_58-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> It also ranked in the top 10, and was the highest ranked Soviet/Russian film in every <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll between 1952 and 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Man_with_a_Movie_Camera" title="Man with a Movie Camera">Man with a Movie Camera</a></i> (1929) was voted the eighth greatest film ever made in the British Film Institute's 2012 <i><a href="/wiki/Sight_%26_Sound" title="Sight &amp; Sound">Sight &amp; Sound</a></i> poll.<sup id="cite_ref-The_50_Greatest_Films_of_All_Time_Sight_&amp;_Sound_147-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_50_Greatest_Films_of_All_Time_Sight_&amp;_Sound-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Mirror_(1975_film)" title="The Mirror (1975 film)">The Mirror</a></i> (1975) ranked 9th in the 2012 <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> directors' poll.<sup id="cite_ref-Directors’_top_100_BFI_148-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Directors’_top_100_BFI-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><i>See also <a href="#Russia">Russia</a>, above</i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Spain">Spain</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Spain" title="Cinema of Spain">Cinema of Spain</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Viridiana" title="Viridiana">Viridiana</a></i> (1961) was voted the best Spanish film of all time with 227 votes in a 2016 poll of 350 experts organized by Spanish film magazine <i>Caimán Cuadernos de Cine</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Executioner_(1963_film)" title="The Executioner (1963 film)"><i>El verdugo</i></a> (1963) was voted the best Spanish film of all time with 77 votes in a 1995 poll of 100 critics and film professionals organized by Spanish film magazine <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Nickel_Odeon_(magazine)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Nickel Odeon (magazine) (page does not exist)">Nickel Odeon</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;(<a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nickel_Odeon_(revista)" class="extiw" title="es:Nickel Odeon (revista)">es</a>)</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sri_Lanka">Sri Lanka</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Cinema of Sri Lanka">Cinema of Sri Lanka</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Anantha_Rathriya" title="Anantha Rathriya">Ananta Rathiriya</a></i> (1995) topped the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a>'s user poll of "Top 10 Sri Lankan Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Purahanda_Kaluwara" title="Purahanda Kaluwara">Pura Handa Kaluwara</a></i> (1997) topped the <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a>'s critics' poll of "Top 10 Sri Lankan Films" of all time in 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sweden">Sweden</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Sweden" title="Cinema of Sweden">Cinema of Sweden</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Phantom_Carriage" title="The Phantom Carriage">The Phantom Carriage</a></i> (<i>Körkarlen</i>, 1921) was voted the best Swedish film of all time with 30 votes in a poll of 50 film critics and academics conducted by film magazine <i>FLM</i> in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Persona_(film)" class="mw-redirect" title="Persona (film)">Persona</a></i> (1966) reached the highest position (number 5 in 1972) of any Swedish film on any of <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i>'s lists of greatest films of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Taiwan">Taiwan</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Taiwan" title="Cinema of Taiwan">Cinema of Taiwan</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/A_City_of_Sadness" title="A City of Sadness">A City of Sadness</a></i> (<span lang="zh-Hant" title="Chinese language text">悲情城市</span>; 1989) was voted the best Chinese-language film of all time with 73 votes in a 2010 poll of 122 film professionals organized by the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Horse_Film_Festival_and_Awards" title="Golden Horse Film Festival and Awards">Taipei Golden Horse Film Festival</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> It was also number 5, the highest ranked Taiwanese film, on the Hong Kong Film Awards' list of the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_Film_Awards#Best_100_Chinese_Motion_Pictures" class="mw-redirect" title="Hong Kong Film Awards">Best 100 Chinese Motion Pictures</a>, voted by 101 filmmakers, critics, and scholars.<sup id="cite_ref-HKFA_88-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HKFA-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkey">Turkey</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Turkey" title="Cinema of Turkey">Cinema of Turkey</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Yol" title="Yol">Yol</a></i> (1982) was voted the best Turkish film of all time in a 2016 poll of 383 experts organized by Turkish magazine <i>Notos</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> It was also selected as the best Turkish film in a 2003 poll undertaken by Ankara Sinema Derneği (Ankara Association for Cinema Culture) of people interested in cinema professionally.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ukraine">Ukraine</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Ukraine" title="Cinema of Ukraine">Cinema of Ukraine</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Shadows_of_Forgotten_Ancestors" title="Shadows of Forgotten Ancestors">Shadows of Forgotten Ancestors</a></i> (1965) was voted the best Ukrainian film of all time with 30 votes in a 2012 poll of about 100 journalists organized by the Cinema Journalism Bureau of Ukraine and the National Union of Cinematographers of Ukraine.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom">United Kingdom</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Cinema of the United Kingdom">Cinema of the United Kingdom</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Third_Man" title="The Third Man">The Third Man</a></i> (1949) was voted the best British film ever by 1000 industry professionals, academics, and critics in a <a href="/wiki/British_Film_Institute" title="British Film Institute">British Film Institute</a> poll conducted in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Lawrence_of_Arabia_(film)" title="Lawrence of Arabia (film)">Lawrence of Arabia</a></i> (1962) was voted the "best British film of all time" in August 2004 by over 200 respondents in a <i><a href="/wiki/Sunday_Telegraph" class="mw-redirect" title="Sunday Telegraph">Sunday Telegraph</a></i> poll of Britain's leading filmmakers.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Get_Carter" title="Get Carter">Get Carter</a></i> (1971) was voted the best British film ever in a 2003 poll by <i><a href="/wiki/Hotdog_(magazine)" title="Hotdog (magazine)">Hotdog</a></i> magazine.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> It also topped the 2004 poll of 25 film critics conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Total_Film" title="Total Film">Total Film</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Don%27t_Look_Now" title="Don&#39;t Look Now">Don't Look Now</a></i> (1973) was named the best British film in a poll of 150 film industry experts conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/Time_Out_London" class="mw-redirect" title="Time Out London">Time Out London</a></i> in 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Monty_Python_and_the_Holy_Grail" title="Monty Python and the Holy Grail">Monty Python and the Holy Grail</a></i> (1975) was voted the best British picture of all time by 7000 film fans in a 2004 poll by the UK arm of Amazon and Internet Movie Database.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Italian_Job" title="The Italian Job">The Italian Job</a></i> (1969) was voted the best British film in a poll of film fans conducted by Sky Movies HD in 2011 when it received 15% of votes.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> It also topped a 2017 survey by <a href="/wiki/Vue_Cinemas" title="Vue Cinemas">Vue Entertainment</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">United States</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Poster shows Rhett Butler carrying Scarlett O&#39;Hara against a backdrop of the Burning of Atlanta" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg/170px-Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg" width="170" height="246" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg/255px-Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg/340px-Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg 2x" data-file-width="350" data-file-height="506" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Gone_With_The_Wind_1967_re-release.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i><a href="/wiki/Gone_with_the_Wind_(film)" title="Gone with the Wind (film)">Gone with the Wind</a></i> (1939) has topped several US audience polls</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_the_United_States" title="Cinema of the United States">Cinema of the United States</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Gone_with_the_Wind_(film)" title="Gone with the Wind (film)">Gone with the Wind</a></i> (1939) was voted the favorite film of Americans in a poll of 2,279 adults undertaken by <a href="/wiki/Harris_Interactive" class="mw-redirect" title="Harris Interactive">Harris Interactive</a> in 2008,<sup id="cite_ref-Harris_2008_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Harris_2008-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and again in a follow-up poll of 2,276 adults in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-Harris_2014_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Harris_2014-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best American film of all time by 35,000 members of the <a href="/wiki/American_Film_Institute" title="American Film Institute">American Film Institute</a> in 1977.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> It was picked in 2011 as the best film for <i><a href="/wiki/Best_in_Film:_The_Greatest_Movies_of_Our_Time" title="Best in Film: The Greatest Movies of Our Time">Best in Film: The Greatest Movies of Our Time</a></i>, an online poll in which over 500,000 votes were cast. Voters chose from a list of 10 English-language films selected by film industry experts.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Citizen_Kane" title="Citizen Kane">Citizen Kane</a></i> (1941) was selected as the greatest American film in 2015 by sixty-two international film critics surveyed by the BBC.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> It was also ranked top in every <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll between 1962 and 2002, and the directors' poll in 1992 and 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/American_Film_Institute" title="American Film Institute">American Film Institute</a> polled 1,500 film community leaders for the lists <i><a href="/wiki/AFI%27s_100_Years...100_Movies" title="AFI&#39;s 100 Years...100 Movies">100 Years...100 Movies</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/AFI%27s_100_Years...100_Movies_(10th_Anniversary_Edition)" title="AFI&#39;s 100 Years...100 Movies (10th Anniversary Edition)">100 Years...100 Movies (10th Anniversary Edition)</a></i> in 1998 and 2007 respectively, asking voters to choose from a list of 400 nominations. Both polls identified <i><a href="/wiki/Citizen_Kane" title="Citizen Kane">Citizen Kane</a></i> as the best <a href="/wiki/Category:American_films" title="Category:American films">American film</a> ever.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> It was voted the best American film of all time with 156 votes in a 1977 poll of 203 experts from 22 countries (116 Americans and 87 non-Americans). The poll was organized by the <a href="/wiki/Cinematek" title="Cinematek">Royal Belgian Film Archive</a> and titled "The most important and misappreciated American films", and they were looking for subjective choices.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Casablanca_(film)" title="Casablanca (film)">Casablanca</a></i> (1942) was voted the greatest American film by readers of the <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Daily_News" title="Los Angeles Daily News">Los Angeles Daily News</a></i> in 1997.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Vertigo_(film)" title="Vertigo (film)">Vertigo</a></i> (1958) topped the <i>Sight &amp; Sound</i> critics' poll in 2012 with 191 votes.<sup id="cite_ref-S&amp;S_1-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-S&amp;S-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Godfather" title="The Godfather">The Godfather</a></i> (1972) was selected as the greatest film by 2,120 industry professionals in a <a href="/wiki/Hollywood" title="Hollywood">Hollywood</a> survey undertaken by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Hollywood_Reporter" title="The Hollywood Reporter">The Hollywood Reporter</a></i> in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-hollywood_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hollywood-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Uruguay">Uruguay</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Uruguay" title="Cinema of Uruguay">Cinema of Uruguay</a></div>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Whisky_(film)" title="Whisky (film)"><i>Whisky</i></a> (2004) was voted the best Uruguayan film of all time by 22 members of the <a href="/wiki/Category:Uruguayan_Film_Critics_Association_Awards" title="Category:Uruguayan Film Critics Association Awards">Uruguayan Film Critics Association</a> in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Venezuela">Venezuela</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cinema_of_Venezuela" title="Cinema of Venezuela">Cinema of Venezuela</a></div>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/El_Pez_que_Fuma" title="El Pez que Fuma">El Pez que Fuma</a></i> (1977) was voted the best Venezuelan film of all time with 22 votes in a 1987 poll of 29 experts organized by <i>Imagen</i> magazine.<sup id="cite_ref-Fundación_Cinemateca_Nacional_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fundación_Cinemateca_Nacional-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> It was also voted the best Venezuelan film of all time with 33 votes in a 2016 poll of 41 experts organized by the <a href="/wiki/Cinemateca_Nacional_de_Venezuela" title="Cinemateca Nacional de Venezuela">Fundación Cinemateca Nacional</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Fundación_Cinemateca_Nacional_174-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fundación_Cinemateca_Nacional-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
